# Iteration 012: GAP ANALYSIS - REFACTORS

## Focus
GAP ANALYSIS - REFACTORS: Should we refactor or change direction on any existing features? Architecture changes?

## Findings

### Finding 1: Public should consolidate bootstrap authority instead of adding a parallel wake-up subsystem
- **Source**: [mcp_server.py#L139](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/mcp_server.py#L139), [mcp_server.py#L169](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/mcp_server.py#L169), [layers.py#L369](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/layers.py#L369), [memory-context.ts#L783](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/handlers/memory-context.ts#L783), [memory-context.ts#L863](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/handlers/memory-context.ts#L863), [context-server.ts#L764](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/context-server.ts#L764), [spec-kit-compact-code-graph.js#L323](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/plugins/spec-kit-compact-code-graph.js#L323)
- **What it does**: MemPalace makes `mempalace_status` double as health check plus behavior bootstrap by returning the protocol and AAAK spec, and its `MemoryStack` keeps wake-up, recall, search, and status in one surface. Public currently spreads startup/recovery semantics across `memory_context` resume heuristics, context-server bootstrap instructions, and compaction transport injection.
- **Why it matters for us**: If we add a MemPalace-style wake-up layer as a separate feature, we risk creating another authority surface on top of `session_bootstrap`, `session_resume`, and `memory_context`. The cleaner direction is to refactor current bootstrap behavior so one Public surface owns startup semantics and the others delegate.
- **Recommendation**: adopt now
- **Impact**: high

### Finding 2: Public should shift compaction resilience from transport enrichment toward enforced save checkpoints
- **Source**: [mempal_save_hook.sh#L4](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/hooks/mempal_save_hook.sh#L4), [mempal_save_hook.sh#L143](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/hooks/mempal_save_hook.sh#L143), [mempal_precompact_hook.sh#L7](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/hooks/mempal_precompact_hook.sh#L7), [mempal_precompact_hook.sh#L71](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/hooks/mempal_precompact_hook.sh#L71), [generate-context.js#L85](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/scripts/dist/memory/generate-context.js#L85), [memory-save.ts#L1273](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/handlers/memory-save.ts#L1273), [save-quality-gate.ts#L526](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/lib/validation/save-quality-gate.ts#L526), [spec-kit-compact-code-graph.js#L396](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/plugins/spec-kit-compact-code-graph.js#L396)
- **What it does**: MemPalace’s stop hook blocks every N exchanges and its pre-compact hook always blocks, telling the agent to save before context loss. Public’s compaction plugin currently injects transport context, while Public’s save path already has a stronger JSON-primary contract, preflight validation, and metadata quality checks.
- **Why it matters for us**: The next architectural step for Public should not be “pack more into compaction transport.” It should be “trigger the existing validated save path before compaction or long sessions end.” That reuses our strongest write hygiene instead of adding a second, looser preservation path.
- **Recommendation**: adopt now
- **Impact**: high

### Finding 3: Taxonomy should stay a browse-and-narrow aid, not become the core retrieval router
- **Source**: [README.md#L62](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/README.md#L62), [README.md#L231](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/mcp_server.py#L231), [README.md#L245](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/README.md#L245), [BENCHMARKS.md#L604](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/benchmarks/BENCHMARKS.md#L604), [BENCHMARKS.md#L615](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/benchmarks/BENCHMARKS.md#L615), [memory-context.ts#L1142](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/handlers/memory-context.ts#L1142)
- **What it does**: MemPalace’s browse surfaces are real and useful, but its own docs now admit the “+34% palace boost” framing was misleading, and its benchmark history shows taxonomy-first routing can crater recall: global LLM routing hit 34.2% R@5, while even the better summary-based room routing still trails the hybrid no-rooms baseline.
- **Why it matters for us**: Public should not refactor `memory_search` or `memory_context` into room-first retrieval. If we add taxonomy, it should help an agent orient or narrow after the fact, while core ranking stays query-led and hybrid.
- **Recommendation**: reject
- **Impact**: high

### Finding 4: Public should reject a separate L0/L1/L2/L3 engine and express wake-up behavior as profiles on the existing retrieval stack
- **Source**: [searcher.py#L21](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/searcher.py#L21), [searcher.py#L93](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/searcher.py#L93), [layers.py#L76](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/layers.py#L76), [layers.py#L185](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/layers.py#L185), [layers.py#L250](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/layers.py#L250), [layers.py#L489](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/layers.py#L489), [memory-context.ts#L439](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/handlers/memory-context.ts#L439), [memory-context.ts#L1322](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/handlers/memory-context.ts#L1322)
- **What it does**: MemPalace’s layer stack is conceptually neat, but it duplicates search/filter logic already present in `searcher.py`, emits formatted text rather than one authoritative structured result shape, and still uses rough token heuristics (`len(...) // 4`). Public already has profile-aware orchestration and budget enforcement in `memory_context`.
- **Why it matters for us**: For Public, a separate wake-up engine would duplicate ranking, result formatting, and token-budget logic we already solved elsewhere. If we want L0/L1-like behavior, it should be expressed as an existing `memory_context`/`session_bootstrap` profile, not as a parallel retrieval subsystem.
- **Recommendation**: reject
- **Impact**: medium

### Finding 5: Public should preserve its modular handler architecture and not absorb new memory features into a single giant server file
- **Source**: [mcp_server.py#L1](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/mcp_server.py#L1), [mcp_server.py#L590](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/mcp_server.py#L590), [mcp_server.py#L848](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/mcp_server.py#L848), [memory-context.ts#L1078](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/handlers/memory-context.ts#L1078), [memory-save.ts#L1273](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/handlers/memory-save.ts#L1273), [save-quality-gate.ts#L602](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/lib/validation/save-quality-gate.ts#L602), [context-server.ts#L1652](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/context-server.ts#L1652)
- **What it does**: MemPalace’s `mcp_server.py` owns tool registration, bootstrap text, drawer writes, KG writes, diary writes, and JSON-RPC dispatch in one file. Public splits orchestration, retrieval, save validation, and server lifecycle into dedicated modules.
- **Why it matters for us**: The next wave of ideas here is taxonomy, hooks, and maybe identity UX. A monolithic merge would make write authority, governance, and review harder. The safer direction is to add any new capabilities as bounded handlers layered on top of the existing validated save/search contracts.
- **Recommendation**: adopt now
- **Impact**: medium

## Assessment
- New information ratio: 0.72
- Questions addressed: bootstrap authority, compaction-survival strategy, taxonomy routing risk, wake-up layering reuse, modularity vs monolith
- Questions answered: the main refactor is consolidation, not expansion; Public should centralize bootstrap/save authority, keep taxonomy auxiliary, and resist adding a parallel wake-up engine or monolithic memory server

## Reflection
- What worked: tracing MemPalace’s README corrections against the actual Python implementation and then comparing those mechanics directly to Public’s live bootstrap, save, and compaction code made the real architectural tradeoffs stand out quickly
- What did not work: the phase root currently only contains `phase-research-prompt.md`, so the brief’s expected Level 3 root docs are not present even though `validate.sh --strict` still passed as inferred Level 1; I also could not run the write-based `spec_kit:deep-research`, report updates, or memory save steps in this read-only sandbox

## Recommended Next Focus
Create a narrow Public-side refactor packet around authority surfaces: make one bootstrap owner, make one validated hook-to-save path, and treat taxonomy as a browse overlay that never outranks hybrid query retrieval.

# Iteration 012: GAP ANALYSIS - REFACTORS

- **Recommendation**: reject
- **Impact**: high

### Finding 4: Public should reject a separate L0/L1/L2/L3 engine and express wake-up behavior as profiles on the existing retrieval stack
- **Source**: [searcher.py#L21](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/searcher.py#L21), [searcher.py#L93](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/searcher.py#L93), [layers.py#L76](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/layers.py#L76), [layers.py#L185](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/layers.py#L185), [layers.py#L250](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/layers.py#L250), [layers.py#L489](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/layers.py#L489), [memory-context.ts#L439](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/handlers/memory-context.ts#L439), [memory-context.ts#L1322](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/handlers/memory-context.ts#L1322)
- **What it does**: MemPalace’s layer stack is conceptually neat, but it duplicates search/filter logic already present in `searcher.py`, emits formatted text rather than one authoritative structured result shape, and still uses rough token heuristics (`len(...) // 4`). Public already has profile-aware orchestration and budget enforcement in `memory_context`.
- **Why it matters for us**: For Public, a separate wake-up engine would duplicate ranking, result formatting, and token-budget logic we already solved elsewhere. If we want L0/L1-like behavior, it should be expressed as an existing `memory_context`/`session_bootstrap` profile, not as a parallel retrieval subsystem.
- **Recommendation**: reject
- **Impact**: medium

### Finding 5: Public should preserve its modular handler architecture and not absorb new memory features into a single giant server file
- **Source**: [mcp_server.py#L1](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/mcp_server.py#L1), [mcp_server.py#L590](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/mcp_server.py#L590), [mcp_server.py#L848](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/specs/system-spec-kit/999-hybrid-rag-fusion-upgrade/001-research-hybrid-rag-fusion-systems/005-mempalace/external/mempalace/mcp_server.py#L848), [memory-context.ts#L1078](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/handlers/memory-context.ts#L1078), [memory-save.ts#L1273](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/handlers/memory-save.ts#L1273), [save-quality-gate.ts#L602](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/lib/validation/save-quality-gate.ts#L602), [context-server.ts#L1652](/Users/michelkerkmeester/MEGA/Development/Code_Environment/Public/.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/context-server.ts#L1652)
- **What it does**: MemPalace’s `mcp_server.py` owns tool registration, bootstrap text, drawer writes, KG writes, diary writes, and JSON-RPC dispatch in one file. Public splits orchestration, retrieval, save validation, and server lifecycle into dedicated modules.
- **Why it matters for us**: The next wave of ideas here is taxonomy, hooks, and maybe identity UX. A monolithic merge would make write authority, governance, and review harder. The safer direction is to add any new capabilities as bounded handlers layered on top of the existing validated save/search contracts.
- **Recommendation**: adopt now
- **Impact**: medium

## Assessment
- New information ratio: 0.72
- Questions addressed: bootstrap authority, compaction-survival strategy, taxonomy routing risk, wake-up layering reuse, modularity vs monolith
- Questions answered: the main refactor is consolidation, not expansion; Public should centralize bootstrap/save authority, keep taxonomy auxiliary, and resist adding a parallel wake-up engine or monolithic memory server

## Reflection
- What worked: tracing MemPalace’s README corrections against the actual Python implementation and then comparing those mechanics directly to Public’s live bootstrap, save, and compaction code made the real architectural tradeoffs stand out quickly
- What did not work: the phase root currently only contains `phase-research-prompt.md`, so the brief’s expected Level 3 root docs are not present even though `validate.sh --strict` still passed as inferred Level 1; I also could not run the write-based `spec_kit:deep-research`, report updates, or memory save steps in this read-only sandbox

## Recommended Next Focus
Create a narrow Public-side refactor packet around authority surfaces: make one bootstrap owner, make one validated hook-to-save path, and treat taxonomy as a browse overlay that never outranks hybrid query retrieval.
